inet-henge用のjinja2テンプレート読み込み¶

In [5]:
#template demo.j2
{
  "nodes": [
{% for router in Routerlist %}
    {
      "meta": {
{% if data.targetrouter == router %}
        "target": "[ TARGET ]"
{% endif %}
      },
     "name": "AS{{ ASlist[loop.index0] }}-{{ router }}",  "icon": "./images/router.png"
{% if loop.last %}
    }
{% else %}
    },
{% endif %}
{% endfor %}
  ],
  "links": [
{% for router in data.node | selectattr("peeraddress", "defined") | list%}
{% set peerAS =  data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', router.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | list %}
{% set peerrouter =  data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', router.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='name' ) | list %}
{% set MED =  data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', router.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='MED' ) | list %}
{% set ASPath =  data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', router.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='ASPath' ) | list %}
{% if not loop.first %}
    },
{% endif %}
    {
      "source": "AS{{ router.AS }}-{{ router.name }}",
{% if data.targetrouter == router.name %}
      "target": "AS{{ peerAS[0] }}-{{ peerrouter[0] }}",
      "meta": {
        "address": {
          "source": "--------{{ router.address }}--------",
          "target": "--------{{ router.peeraddress }}--------"
        },
          "MED/LP/ASPath": "MED:{{ MED[0] | default('default') }}/LP:{{ router.LP | default('default') }}/ASPrepend:{{ ASPath[0] | default(default) }}"
        }
{% else %}
      "target": "AS{{ peerAS[0] }}-{{ peerrouter[0] }}"
{% endif %}

{% endfor %}
    }
  ]
}

  dest='/home/notebook/notebooks/inet-henge/example/index.html'
  state=present
  backrefs=yes
  regexp='{{ item.regexp }}'
  line='{{ item.line }}'
with_items:
- regexp: "^(.*)diagram.init(.*)$"
  line: "   diagram.init('target', 'address', 'MED/LP/ASPath');"

すべて許可するroute-policy作成¶












In [13]:



    


#task
name: |
   - route-policy ALLPASS
   - pass
   - exit
iosxr_config:
  commands:
   - pass
   - exit
  parents: route-policy ALLPASS
  match: none
register: result


























TASK [- route-policy ALLPASS
- pass
- exit
] ***********************************
changed: [10.0.0.109] => {
    "commands": [
        "route-policy ALLPASS", 
        "pass", 
        "exit"
    ]
}























MEDをつけるroute-policyを作成¶












In [14]:



    


name: |
   - route-policy med{{ item.MED }}-out
   - set med {{ item.MED }}
   - end-policy
iosxr_config:
  lines: 
   - set med {{ item.MED }}
   - end-policy
  parents: route-policy med{{ item.MED }}-out
  force: yes
register: result
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node | selectattr('MED', 'defined') | list }}"

Vlan I/Fを作成する¶












In [15]:



    


#task
name: |
   - interface {{ item.ifname }}
   - mtu {{ data.mtu }}
   - dot1q native vlan 1
   - no shutdown
iosxr_config:
  lines: 
   - dot1q vlan {{ item.vlan }}
   - no shutdown
   - ipv4 address {{ item.address }}/{{ data.defaultmask }}
   - mtu {{ item.mtu }}
  parents: interface {{ item.ifname }}.{{ item.vlan }}
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node }}"
register: result

- dot1q native vlan 1

BGPの設定追加①(MEDをつけるピア向け)¶












In [16]:



    


#task
name: |
   - bgp router-id 2.2.2.2
   - address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} remote-as {{ data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', item.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy ALLPASS in
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy med{{ item.MED }}-out out
iosxr_config:
  lines: 
   - bgp router-id 2.2.2.2
   - address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} remote-as {{ data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', item.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy ALLPASS in
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy med{{ item.MED }}-out out
  parents: router bgp {{ item.AS }}
register: result
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node | selectattr('MED', 'defined') | list}}"

#task
name: |
   - bgp router-id 2.2.2.2
   - address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} remote-as {{ data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', router.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='MED' ) | max }}
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy ALLPASS in
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy med{{ item.MED }}-out out
iosxr_config:
  lines: 
   - bgp router-id 2.2.2.2
   - address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} remote-as {{ data.node | selectattr('address', 'match', item.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy ALLPASS in
   - neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} address-family ipv4 unicast route-policy ALLPASS out
  parents: router bgp {{ item.AS }}
register: result
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node | selectattr('MED', 'undefined') | list}}"

BGPのセッションクリア¶












In [18]:



    


name: clear bgp ipv4 unicast {{ item.peeraddress }} soft out  
iosxr_command:
  commands:
   - clear bgp ipv4 unicast {{ item.peeraddress }} soft out
register: result
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node | selectattr('peeraddress', 'defined') | list}}"

Router-ID設定¶












In [20]:



    


#task
name: |
   - set routing-options router-id 3.3.3.3
   - set routing-options autonomous-system {{ data.node | selectattr('mgmtaddress', 'match', ansible_host ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}
connection: netconf
junos_config:
  lines: 
   - set routing-options router-id 3.3.3.3
   - set routing-options autonomous-system {{ data.node | selectattr('mgmtaddress', 'match', ansible_host ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}

Vlan I/F作成¶












In [21]:



    


#task
name: create vlan interfaces
connection: netconf
junos_config:
  lines: 
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} flexible-vlan-tagging
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} unit {{ item.vlan }} vlan-id {{ item.vlan }}
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} unit {{ item.vlan }} family inet address {{ item.address }}/{{ data.defaultmask }}
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} unit {{ item.vlan }} family inet mtu {{ item.mtu | default("1500") }}
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node }}"
register: result

#task
name: |
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} type external
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} hold-time 90
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} family inet unicast
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} export redist-direct
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} peer-as {{ data.node  | selectattr('address', 'match', item.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}

Vlan I/Fの作成¶












In [27]:



    


#task
name: create vlan interfaces
connection: network_cli
junos_command:
  commands:
   - configure
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} flexible-vlan-tagging
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} unit {{ item.vlan }} vlan-id {{ item.vlan }}
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} unit {{ item.vlan }} family inet address {{ item.address }}/{{ data.defaultmask }}
   - set interfaces {{ item.ifname }} unit {{ item.vlan }} family inet mtu {{ item.mtu }}
   - commit
   - exit
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node }}"
register: result

   - set routing-options autonomous-system {{ data.node | selectattr('mgmtaddress', 'match', ansible_host ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}

   - set routing-options autonomous-system {{ data.node | selectattr('mgmtaddress', 'match', ansible_host ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}

   - exit

   - set policy-options policy-statement LP-{{ item.LP }} term 1 then local-preference {{ item.LP }}
   - set policy-options policy-statement LP-{{ item.LP }} term 1 then accept

   - configure

BGP設定の投入¶












In [30]:



    


#task
name: |
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} type external
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} hold-time 90
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} family inet unicast
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} peer-as {{ data.node  | selectattr('address', 'match', item.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} import LP-{{ item.LP }} 

connection: network_cli
junos_command:
  commands:
   - configure
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} type external
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} hold-time 90
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} family inet unicast
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} peer-as {{ data.node  | selectattr('address', 'match', item.peeraddress ) | map(attribute='AS' ) | max }}
   - set protocols bgp group {{ item.peeraddress }} neighbor {{ item.peeraddress }} import LP-{{ item.LP }}   
   - commit
   - exit
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node | selectattr('LP', 'defined') | list }}"
register: result

設定投入後の正常性確認¶
















Junosルータから受信している経路の一つを選択し、想定どおり(metrix 100)の経路を選定しているかを確認¶












In [32]:



    


#task
name: show route {{  data.network[3]["address"]  }}
junos_command:
  commands:
   - show route {{ data.network[3]["address"] }}
register: result


























TASK [show route 172.16.4.0/24] ************************************************

結果(OKかNGか等)¶
















想定通りのMED100/LocalPref300の経路が選択されているのでOK¶
















デモ向け設定削除¶












In [34]:



    


#task
name: |
   - delete protocols bgp
   - delete interface xe-0/0/0:0

connection: network_cli
junos_command:
  commands:
   - configure
   - delete protocols bgp
   - delete interface xe-0/0/0:0
   - commit
   - exit
when: ansible_host == item.mgmtaddress
with_items:
  - "{{ data.node | selectattr('LP', 'defined') | list }}"
register: result
